  var _ajax = new XMLHttpRequest();

  _ajax.open('GET', url, true);
  _ajax.send();
  _ajax.onload = function () {
    var div = document.createElement('div');
    div.hidden = true;
    div.innerHTML = _ajax.responseText;
    document.body.insertBefore(div, document.body.childNodes[0]);
  };
}
